  if [ -f $i ]; then \
    j=`echo $i | sed -e 's/-new//'`; \
    k=`echo $j | sed 's&^&mips-openwrt-linux-musl-&'`; \
    if [ "/home/runner/work/openwrt-rebuilder/openwrt-rebuilder/rebuild/staging_dir/toolchain-mips_24kc_gcc-7.5.0_musl/initial/bin/$k" != "/home/runner/work/openwrt-rebuilder/openwrt-rebuilder/rebuild/staging_dir/toolchain-mips_24kc_gcc-7.5.0_musl/initial/mips-openwrt-linux-musl/bin/$j" ]; then \
      rm -f /home/runner/work/openwrt-rebuilder/openwrt-rebuilder/rebuild/staging_dir/toolchain-mips_24kc_gcc-7.5.0_musl/initial/mips-openwrt-linux-musl/bin/$j; \
      ln /home/runner/work/openwrt-rebuilder/openwrt-rebuilder/rebuild/staging_dir/toolchain-mips_24kc_gcc-7.5.0_musl/initial/bin/$k /home/runner/work/openwrt-rebuilder/openwrt-rebuilder/rebuild/staging_dir/toolchain-mips_24kc_gcc-7.5.0_musl/initial/mips-openwrt-linux-musl/bin/$j >/dev/null 2>/dev/null \

  fi; \
done
